View the total value of your investment accounts or the performance of individual stocks and mutual funds over time. Stock splits and cost basis computations are a snap, and current prices can be downloaded automatically.\r\n\r\n∞ REMINDERS\r\nYou can set up a payment schedule for single or recurring transactions so you'll never miss a payment.\r\n\r\n∞ GRAPHS/REPORTS\r\nUse the graphing tool to generate visual reports of your income and expenses. Set the graph type, the date range, and any specific settings for the type of graph you desire. Pop-up balloons display more information about the data being graphed as you move the mouse pointer over different regions of the screen. Graphs can also be printed or saved to PNG image files.\r\n\r\n∞ BUDGETS\r\nSet spending targets for categories per month, week or any other interval. View your up-to-the-minute budget status right in the toolbar, on the home page or in detailed graphs and reports. Use the highly acclaimed \"envelope method\" to specify expenses for each period and your to-the-minute status is shown with over-budget items highlighted. Moneydance will help you set a target and stick to it!\r\n\r\n∞ SYNC\r\nEnable file syncing to share or collaborate on a data file across multiple computers. Whether sharing with your partner or accountant, syncing your data will provide secure efficient access to your accounts from any computer.\r\n\r\n∞ NATURAL LANGUAGE TRANSACTION ENTRY\r\nStart typing a transaction description into the search field and Moneydance will intelligently fill in the details based on natural language date parsing and your history. In addition to OpenDocument formats (.ods, .ots, .sxc and .stc), Excel Editor can open the following spreadsheet formats:\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 97/2000/XP (.xls, .xlw, and .xlt)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 4.x–5.0/95 (.xls, .xlw, and .xlt)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 2003 XML (.xml)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 2007/2010/2013/2016 XML (.xlsx, .xlsm, .xltx, .xltm)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 2007 binary (.xlsb)\r\n•\tLotus 1-2-3 (.wk1, .wks, and .123)\r\n•\tData Interchange Format (.dif)\r\n•\tRich Text Format (.rtf)\r\n•\tText CSV (.csv and .txt)\r\n•\tStarCalc formats (.sdc and .vor)\r\n•\tdBASE (.dbf)\r\n•\tSYLK (.slk)\r\n•\tUnified Office Format spreadsheet (.uos, .uof)\r\n•\t.htm and .html files, including Web page queries\r\n•\tPocket Excel (pxl)\r\n•\tQuattro Pro 6.0 (.wb2)\r\n\t\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.ods and .ots), Ultra XLSX Editor can save in these formats:\r\n•\tOpenOffice.org 1.x Spreadsheet (.sxc)\r\n•\tOpenOffice.org 1.x Spreadsheet Template (.stc)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 2007 - 2019 (.xlsx)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 97/2000/XP (.xls and .xlw)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 97/2000/XP Template (.xlt)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 5.0 and 95 (.xls and .xlw)\r\n•\tMicrosoft Excel 2003 XML (.xml)\r\n•\tData Interchange Format (.dif)\r\n•\tdBase (.dbf)SYLK (.slk)Text CSV (.csv and .txt)\r\n•\tStarCalc 3.0, 4.0, and 5.0 formats (.sdc and .vor)\r\n•\tUnified Office Format spreadsheet (.uos)\r\n•\tHTML Document (OpenOffice.org Calc) (.html and .htm)\r\n•\tPocket Excel (.pxl)\r\n\r\n*** Note: this app does not support Windows 10 S, which was discontinued in March 2018.
